heights = ....
left, right = 0, len(arr) - 1
area = 0
while left < right:
    mh = min(heights[left], heights[right] 
    dif = right - left
    ar = mh * dif
    area = max(area, ar)

        left += 1

        right -= 1

res = [1] * len(nums)
# lets do prefix
pre = 1

    pre *= nums[i]
